 smartphone ko controlmen lekar vah aapke mobile main koi bhi mailaware daal saktaa he taaki aapaki tamaam jaankariyaan or bank tranjaction detail uske paas aasaani se pahunch saken
 What is stagefrightstagefright was first reported in 2003
 yah havers dwaara taiyaar kiya gaya ek bag he jo android divaais ke media processing system par atake karata he
 Once the media processing system is weakened, hackers are controlled in the smartphone via Mp3 or Mp4
 google ne kaha khatarnaak he yah bagagoogle ne is bag kaa khandan 15 agast ko kiya

 Cremation means the last floor of life
 or chita
 
 
 That means the last truth of life
 par jaraa sochen
 
 
 
 agarisi shmashaan main usichitake kareeb koi mehfil sajabaithe or shuru ho jaae shmashaan main dance to use aap kya kahenge?khamosh, gamagin, udhaas or bichbich menchitaaon kii lakadiyon ke chatkhane kii aawaaj amuman kisi bhi shmashaan kaa manzar yaa maahaul kuchaisa hi hota he
 But one night is very special for the crematorium
 ek aisi raat jo shmashaan ke liye raunak kii raat he
 Because this night descends only once a year at this crematorium and that is why this night becomes completely unique from the rest of the 364 nights of the year
 ye ek raat is shmashaan ke liye jashn kii raat he
 On this one night, cremations are also burnt together at this crematorium and steps are also made between ghungroos and fast music
 kaashi ke us shmashanaper jiske bare main ye mashhoor he kiyaha chita par letne vaaleko sidhe moksh miltaa he
 The only cremation in the world where the fire of pyre never cools down
 jahaan laashon kaa aana or chita kaa jalanaa kabhi nahin thamata
 But when the dance started dancing right close to the pyre
 matam ke bich tej sangeet par ladkiyaan thirakane lagen or jab maut kii khaamoshi dance kii masti main badal jaae to phirchaunkna lajimi he
 Now the question arises that why this dance between Chita is fun? Why is a human being allowed to be relieved by funeral pyre even after death? Why are some girls dancing near the pyre in the crematorium? Manikarnika Ghat of Kashi has been witness to both the pyre and the Mahafil
 vahi manikarnika ghat jo sadiyon se maut or moksh kaa bhigavah banataa ayaahai
 Today, this ghat is adorned with a staggering feast filled with fun
 ek aisi mehafil jo jitna daraati he usase kahin zyadahairanakrti he
 What is the truth of this festival, girls dancing near the funeral pyre are the city's bride in the infamous streets of the city
 kal kii nagarvadhu yaniaj keetvayph
 But they are neither forcibly brought here nor are they called on the basis of money
 kaashi ke jis manikarnika ghat par maut ke baadamoksh kii talash main murdonko laayaa jaataa he vahiin par ye tamaam nagarvadhuen jite ji moksh hasil karne aati hai
 The salvation that assures them not to become natives in the next life
 inhen yakeen he ki agar is ek raat ye ji bharke yun hi naachengi to phir agle janm main inhen nagarvadhoo kaa kalankanhin jhelana padegaa
 For him, it gives him the time to get salvation
 saal main ek baar ye mauka aata he caitra navaratri ke aathven din
 And on this day in the Shiva temple next to the crematorium, all the townspeople of the city gather and then dance in front of God
 yahaan aane vaali tamaam nagarvadhuen apane aapako behad khushnaseeb maanati hai
 But at this ghat of Kashi, all these things did not start suddenly
 balki iske peeche ek behad puraani paramparahe
 More disturbing than what is surprising
 shmashaan ke sannaate ke bich nagarvadhuon ke dance kii parampara saikadon saal puraani he
 According to beliefs, famous dancers and artists of that time were invited to present the function in the court of Baba Mashan Nath, built by Raja Man Singh hundreds of years ago, but since this temple was present in the middle of the crematorium So many top artists of the time refused to come here to show their art
 lekin chunki raja ne dance ke is kaarykram kaa elaan puure shahar main karvaa diya tha, lihaaza wo apni baat se peeche nahin hat sakate the
 But the matter had stopped here that when he finally came to dance between the crematorium, who was coming? Time was passing fast in the same turmoil
 lekin kisi ko kuch samaj main nahin aa rahaa tha
 When no one thought of any solution, it was decided that the city dwellers living in the infamous streets of the city should be called to dance in this temple
 upaay kaam kar gaya or nagarvadhuon ne yahaan aakar is mahashmashaan ke bich dance karne kaa nyotaa sweekaar kar liya
 This tradition has been going on since then
 guzarate vakt ke saath jab nagarvadhuon ne apana chola badla to ek baar phir se is parampara ke raste main rode aa gaye
 And to this day, the Bargirl of Mumbai is called to carry on this tradition
 yahi nahin parampara kisi bhi qeemat par chhootane naa paae, iskaa bhi khaas khyaal rakhaa jaataa he
 And for this, all arrangements are made on this very special day of the year
 is aayojan ko zyaada se zyada safal banane ke liye police-prashasan ke numaayindebakaydaais mehfil kaa hissaa banate hai
 The deep roots of this tradition can be gauged from the fact that many foreign tourists coming to Benaras are unable to stop themselves from seeing this special occasion
 yebehad anokhi or chaunkaane valiparampara jitani sach he utana hi sach he in nagarvadhuon kaa vajood jo har jamaane main moksh kii talash main yahaan aata rahaa he
 Tax is charged for burning pyre
 You may not believe it, but every dead person visiting this cremation ground is taxed before putting it on the pyre
 shmashaan ghat par laashon se paise vasuulne ke pichheki ye kahaneebhi kamadilachaspanhin he
 The tradition of paying the price of funeral at Manikarnika Ghat is about three thousand years old
 manyata he ki shmashaan ke rakh rakhaav kaa jimmaa tabhi se dom jati ke haath tha
 Since the Dome caste had no other means of employment then, there was a tradition of donating them on the occasion of cremation
 magar dom tab dah sanskaar kii yun munh maangi keemat nahin maangate the or naa hi paisa kamaane ke galat tareeke apanaate the
 Actually the current phase of tax collection started with the era of Raja Harishchandra
 harishchandra ne tab ek vachan ke tahat apana rajpaat chhod kar dom parivaar ke purvaj kallu dom kii naukari kii thi
 Meanwhile, his son died and he was forced to ask permission for Kallu Dome to cremate his son
 chunki bina daan diye tab bhi antim sanskaar kii ijazat nahin thi lihaaja raja harishchandra ko majabuuran apni patni kii sari kaa ek tukdaa bataur dakshina kallu dom ko dena padaa
 Just then, the tradition of demanding tax in lieu of cremation became stronger
 vahi parampara jiskaa bigadaa hua rup manikarnika ghat par aaj bhi jari he
 Since this profession has now fully taken the shape of a business, the dom family has spread spies on the crematorium
 unki najar shmashaan main aane vaali har shav yatra par rahati he taaki kis party se kitna paisa vasula ja saktaa he iskaa thik thik andaja lagaaya ja sake
 By the way, if the Dom family is to be believed, then in the past, there was no shortage of nobles who looted their wealth
 unka daawa he ki us daur main antim sanskaar ke evaj main unhen raaje rajavaade jameen jaaydaad yahaan tak kii sona-chaandi tak diya karte the
 While for the fixed amount of money, they have to get entangled with the crematorium
 'nach baliye' sijan 8 ke liye jodiya jitod mehnat kar rahi hai
 In such a situation, Sonakshi Sinha, who is seen as the judge of this show, is also going to host the first episode of this show
 lekin lagata he jaj ke taur par in 10 jodiyon ke dance ko jaj karne vaali sonakshi ne pehle hi apni favorit jodi chun lee he

 When asked about the emphasis on feature phones, Aggarwal said, "A large population of the country is still preferring feature phones
" iskaa kaaran logon kii kam aay, smart phone kii unchi keemat, chhate kasbon, gaanvon main network or bijli kii samasya he
 Also, a large section of the villages are still unfamiliar with modern technology and social media platforms
 ’’ yah baat isse sabit hoti he ki desh main basic phone ke bazaar kii vruddhi jahaan 30 pratishat se adhik he vahiin smartphone kii vruddhi 20 pratishat ke aasapaas he
 Keeping this in mind, we are paying special attention to feature phones, but in the coming time, our smartphone will also be emphasized
 ’’ company ke kaarobaar ke bare main puche jane par unhone kaha ki hamaara kaarobaar 2016-17 main badhkar 130 karod rapaye ho jane kaa anumaan he jo 2015-16 main 220 karod rupee tha
 The comments vitaran network ke bare main agarwal ne kaha ki abhi hamaare paas desh bhar main 500 se adhik vitarankarta jude hue hai or ham agle dedh saal main 300 se adhik vitarankarta or jodenge
 Asked about employment, he said that with the commissioning of the new factory, we have plans to appoint 700 people from lower level to higher management levels by the end of the current financial year
 iske saath hamaare kaarybal kii sankhya 1500 ho jaaegi
 The company currently imports parts and assembles mobile handsets, but it now plans to manufacture these devices indigenously
 mukhya rup se feechar phone banane vaali company ne chaalu vitt varsh main 700 naye karmchaariyon kii niyukti or vitarakon kii sankhya badhaakar 800 karne kii bhi yojana banaayi he
 "we currently have two small units in Baddi in Himachal Pradesh where we are assembling three lakh feature phones and smartphones every month," the company's co-founder and managing director Vivek Agarwal told PTI
 hamaari yojana chaalu vitt varsh main ise badhaakar paanch lakh masik or agle vitt varsh tak aath lakh karne kii he
 For this, we are setting up a new factory with an investment of Rs 20 crore, which will start functioning fully from the beginning of the next financial year 2017-18
 ’’ unhone kaha ki yah kaarkaana puri tarah se chaalu hone par ham har maheene aath lakh phone essembel kar sakenge
 Aggarwal said that at the same time we are emphasizing on manufacturing and in the initial phase we will make products like batteries, chargers, ear phones and speakers and in the coming time we will be completely making mobile handsets in accordance with 'make in India' Will manufacture yah sab naye kaarkaane main hoga
 In response to a question, Vivek Aggarwal said that currently the ratio of feature phones and smartphones in our sales is 90:10 and we plan to increase it to 75:25
 feechar phone par itnaa jor dene ke bare main puche jane par agarwal ne kaha, ‘‘desh kii ek badi aabaadi abhi bhi feechar phone pasand kar rahi he
 The reason for this is the low income of the people, the high cost of smart phones, the network and power problems in the towns, villages
 saath hi gaanvon main abhi bhi ek bada tabaka aadhunik takanic or soshal media platform se aparichit hai
 "this proves that while the basic phone market growth in the country is more than 30 percent, the growth of the smartphone is around 20 percent
" isi ko dhyaan main rakhkar ham feechar phone par vishesh dhyaan de rahe hai lekin aane vaale samay main hamaara smartphone par bhi jor hoga
 When asked about the business of the company, he said that our business is expected to increase to Rs 130 crore in 2016-17, from Rs 220 crore in 2015-16
 tippaniyan Regarding the distribution network, Agarwal said that we have more than 500 distributors connected across the country right now and we will add more than 300 distributors in the next year and a half
 rojgaar ke bare main puche jane par unhone kaha ki naye kaarkaane ke chaalu hone ke saath hamaari chaalu vitt varsh ke ant tak nichle str se lekar ucch prabandhan staron par 700 logon ko niyukt karne kii yojana he

 (input bhashaa se) Cabinet approval of the Citizenship Amendment Bill will be introduced in Parliament soon
 Citizenship Bill: There are many parties in the northeast opposing the bill
 The National Government Register (NRC) did not even stand up in the Northeast that the Central Government brought the Citizenship Amendment Bill
 buudhvaar ko yah bill rajyasabha se bhi paas ho gaya
 It was also passed by the Lok Sabha on Monday
 bill main badlaav ke saath hi bharat main basane vaale sharnaarthiyon ko milane vaali naagarikta ke kai niyam badal jaaenge, jiskaa vipaksh virodh kar rahaa he
 Understand what is special in this bill, on which opposition is opposing and what changes are going to happen
 
 
 1
 What is the Citizenship Amendment Bill? The bill that has been passed by Parliament will change the Citizenship Act 1955
 iske tahat bangladesh, pakistan, afghanistan samet aas paas ke deshon se bharat main aane vaale hindu, sikh, buddha, jain, parsi dharm vaale logon ko naagarikta di jaaegi
 2
 kaise bharat kii naagarikta milanaa hoga aasaan?is bill ke kanoon main tabdeel hone ke barfghanistan, bangladesh, pakistan jaise deshon se jo gaiyr-muslim sharnaarthi bharat aaenge, unhen yahaan kii naagarikta milanaa aasaan ho jayega
 For this, they have to spend at least 6 years in India
 pehle naagarikta dene kaa paimaana 11 saal se adhik tha
 3
 bill par kis baat kaa virodh ho rahaa he?is bill ko lekar vipaksh centre sarkaar ko gher rahaa he, jisamen mukhya virodh dharm ko lekar he
 In the new amendment bill, it is being decided to give citizenship easily to people of other religions except Muslims
 vipaksh isi baat ko uthaa rahaa he or modi sarkaar ke is faisle ko dharm ke aadhaar par baantne vaala bataa rahaa he
 4
 endie main hi hua bill kaa virodh?modi sarkaar ke liye sabase badi mushkil ye rahi ki is bill kaa virodh uske ghatak dal endie main hi hua
 The Asom Gana Parishad, a partner of the Bharatiya Janata Party in the Northeast, openly opposed the bill, saying that it had not spoken to its allies before bringing the bill, while it was promised to speak
 assam gana parishad assam sarkaar main bijepi ke saath rahi
 Union Home Minister Amit Shah will introduce Bill 5
 purvottar main kyon hamalavar hai log?abhi kuch samay pehle hi neshnal register of citigen ko lekar assam samet purvottar ke anya rajyon main baari virodh hua tha
 Soon after the NRC, the Citizenship Amendment Bill (CAB) was introduced, which is opposed
 north east students orgenigeshan kii aguwai main purvottar ke kai chaatr sanghathanon ne is bill kaa virodh kiya
 Click this and read: What is the Citizenship Amendment Bill and why it is opposed 6
 kya bijepi ko hoga raajnneetik laabh?assam, bengal jaise rajyon main sharnaarthiyon kaa mudda kaaphi haaavee rahaa he
 Before the assembly elections in Assam or the Lok Sabha elections in the country, the BJP had vigorously raised the issue of NRC, which also benefited them
 ab jab pashchim bengal main chunaav aane vaale hai to usase pehle ek baar phir CAB bill par bhaajapa aakraamak ho gai he
 In such a situation, political matters are also being extracted regarding this bill
 7
 Passed in Lok Sabha but 
 
 is bill ko sabase pehle 2016 main loksabhaa main pesh kiya gaya tha, jiske baad ise sansadeey cameti ke hawaale kar diya gaya
 Earlier this year, the bill was passed in the Lok Sabha but was stuck in the Rajya Sabha
 haalanki, loksabhaa kaa kaarykaal khatm hone ke saath hi bill bhi khatm ho gaya
 But this time the Modi government managed to get it passed by both the Lok Sabha and the Rajya Sabha
 desh main maujuuda raajnneetik halchal ke bich ek baar phir tisare morche kii siyasat jor pakadati dikh rahi he
 Samajwadi Party President Mulayam Singh Yadav has said that in 2014 only the Third Front government will be formed
 mulaayam ne kaha ki madhyavadhi chunaav ke liye unki party jimmedaar nahin hogi
